v\xc3\xb9ng c\xc3\xa1ch ly, ch\xc6\xb0a th\xe1\xbb\x83 d\xe1\xbb\xb1 thi \xc4\x91\xe1\xbb\xa3t 1.</p></div></div></div><div class="col-sm-6 col-md-4"><div class="thumbnail"><a
